 1900|"Howard Hathaway Aiken":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/howard-hathaway-aiken Howard Hathaway Aiken was born on 9 March 1900 in Hoboken, New Jersey, USA. Howard Aiken was a pioneer designer of early computers. Howard Hathaway Aiken died on 14 March 1973 in St Louis, Missouri, USA./||
 1900|"Frederick Bath":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/frederick-bath Frederick Bath was born on 10 September 1900 in Islington, London, England. Frederick Bath graduated from Bristol and Cambridge and held posts at King's College London, University College Dundee, St Andrews and Edinburgh. He worked in Geometry. Frederick Bath died on 2 September 1982 in Dartmouth, Devon, England./||
 1900|"John Charles Burkill":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/john-charles-burkill John Charles Burkill was born on 1 February 1900 in Holt, Norfolk, England. J C Burkill was an English mathematician who worked on analysis and introduced the Burkill integral. He is best-known for his analysis textbooks. John Charles Burkill died on 6 April 1993 in Sheffield, England./||
 1900|"Dame Mary Lucy Cartwright":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/dame-mary-lucy-cartwright Dame Mary Lucy Cartwright was born on 17 December 1900 in Aynho, Northamptonshire, England. Mary Cartwright was the first woman mathematician to be elected to the Royal Society. She became Mistress of Girton College, Cambridge. Dame Mary Lucy Cartwright died on 3 April 1998 in Cambridge, England./||
 1900|"Wilhelm Cauer":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/wilhelm-cauer Wilhelm Cauer was born on 24 June 1900 in Berlin, Germany. Wilhelm Cauer died on 22 April 1945 in Berlin, Germany./||
 1900|"Edward Foyle Collingwood":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/edward-foyle-collingwood Edward Foyle Collingwood was born on 17 January 1900 in Alnwick, Northumberland, England. Edward Foyle Collingwood died on 25 October 1970 in Alnwick, Northumberland, England./||
 1900|"Gertrude Mary Cox":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/gertrude-mary-cox Gertrude Mary Cox was born on 13 January 1900 in Dayton, Iowa, USA. Gertrude Mary Cox died on 17 October 1978 in Durham, North Carolina, USA./||
 1900|"Haskell Brooks Curry":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/haskell-brooks-curry Haskell Brooks Curry was born on 12 September 1900 in Millis, Massachusetts, USA. Haskell Curry worked in mathematical logic with particular interest in the theory of formal systems and processes. Haskell Brooks Curry died on 1 September 1982 in State College, Pennsylvania , USA./||
 1900|"David van Dantzig":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/david-van-dantzig David van Dantzig was born on 23 September 1900 in Amsterdam, Netherlands. David van Dantzig died on 22 July 1959 in Amsterdam, Netherlands./||
 1900|"Hendrik Douwe Kloosterman":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/hendrik-douwe-kloosterman Hendrik Douwe Kloosterman was born on 9 April 1900 in Rottevalle, The Netherlands. Hendrik Douwe Kloosterman died in 1968 in Leiden, The Netherlands./||
 1900|"Mikhail Alekseevich Lavrentev":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/mikhail-alekseevich-lavrentev Mikhail Alekseevich Lavrentev was born on 19 November 1900 in Kazan, Russia. Mikhail Lavrent'ev is remembered for an outstanding book on conformal mappings and he made many important contributions to that topic. Mikhail Alekseevich Lavrentev died on 15 October 1980 in Moscow, Russia./||
 1900|"Wolfgang Ernst Pauli":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/wolfgang-ernst-pauli Wolfgang Ernst Pauli was born on 25 April 1900 in Vienna, Austria. Wolfgang Pauli won a Nobel prize for his work on quantum mechanics. Wolfgang Ernst Pauli died on 15 December 1958 in Zürich, Switzerland./||
 1900|"Abraham Ezechiel Plessner":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/abraham-ezechiel-plessner Abraham Ezechiel Plessner was born on 13 February 1900 in Lódz, Russian Empire (now Poland). Abraham Ezechiel Plessner died on 18 April 1961 in Moscow, USSR./||
 1900|"László Rédei":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/laszlo-redei László Rédei was born on 15 November 1900 in Rákoskeresztur, Budapest, Hungary. László Rédei died on 21 November 1980 in Budapest, Hungary./||
 1900|"George Eugene Uhlenbeck":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/george-eugene-uhlenbeck George Eugene Uhlenbeck was born on 6 December 1900 in Batavia, Java (now Jakarta, Indonesia). George Eugene Uhlenbeck died on 31 October 1988 in Boulder, Colorado, USA./||
 1900|"Gheorghe Vrănceanu":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/gheorghe-vranceanu Gheorghe Vrănceanu was born on 30 June 1900 in Valea Hogii, Vaslui, Romania. Gheorghe Vrănceanu died on 27 April 1979 in Bucharest, Romania./||
 1900|"William John Youden":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/william-john-youden William John Youden was born on 12 April 1900 in Townsville, Australia. William John Youden died on 31 March 1971 in Washington, D.C., USA./||
 1900|"Antoni Szczepan Zygmund":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/antoni-szczepan-zygmund Antoni Szczepan Zygmund was born on 25 December 1900 in Warsaw, Russian Empire (now Poland). Zygmund's work in harmonic analysis has application in the theory of waves and vibrations. He also did major work in Fourier analysis and its application to partial differential equations. Antoni Szczepan Zygmund died on 30 May 1992 in Chicago, Illinois, USA./||
 1901|"Naum Il'ich Akhiezer":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/naum-il'ich-akhiezer/||
 1901|"Nina Karlovna Bari":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/nina-karlovna-bari Nina Karlovna Bari was born on 19 November 1901 in Moscow, Russia. Nina Karlovna Bari died on 15 July 1961 in Moscow, Russia./||
 1901|"Raj Chandra Bose":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/raj-chandra-bose Raj Chandra Bose was born on 19 June 1901 in Hoshangabad, Madhya Pradesh, India. Raj Chandra Bose died on 31 October 1987 in Fort Collins, Colorado, USA./||
 1901|"Richard Dagobert Brauer":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/richard-dagobert-brauer Richard Dagobert Brauer was born on 10 February 1901 in Berlin-Charlottenburg, Germany. Brauer became interested in work on group characters. He formulated a method to classify all finite simple groups and spent the rest of his life working on this problem. Richard Dagobert Brauer died on 17 April 1977 in Belmont, Massachusetts, USA./||
 1901|"Edward Thomas Copson":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/edward-thomas-copson Edward Thomas Copson was born on 21 August 1901 in Coventry, England. Edward Copson was an expert on Complex Analysis and was Regius Professor of Mathematics at St Andrews from 1950 until 1969. Edward Thomas Copson died on 16 February 1980 in St Andrews, Fife, Scotland./||
 1901|"Winifred Margaret Deans":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/winifred-margaret-deans Winifred Margaret Deans was born on 9 October 1901 in New Milton, Hampshire, England. Winifred Deans graduated from Aberdeen and Cambridge. After a period in teaching she joined a Scottish publishing company and translated many important German scientific texts for them. After World War II she worked at the Commonwealth Bureau of Animal Nutrition in Aberdeen. Winifred Margaret Deans died on 7 Jun 1990 in Milltimber, Peterculter, Aberdeenshire, Scotland./||
 1901|"Machgielis Euwe":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/machgielis-euwe Machgielis Euwe was born on 20 May 1901 in Watergraafsmeer, near Amsterdam, Netherlands. Machgielis Euwe died on 26 November 1981 in Amsterdam, Holland./||
 1901|"Luigi Fantappiè":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/luigi-fantappie Luigi Fantappiè was born on 15 September 1901 in Viterbo, Italy. Luigi Fantappiè died on 28 July 1956 in Bagnaia, near Viterbo, Italy./||
 1901|"Enrico Fermi":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/enrico-fermi Enrico Fermi was born on 29 September 1901 in Rome, Italy. Enrico Fermi was an Italian physicist who created the world's first nuclear reactor. He made important contributions to the development of quantum theory, nuclear and particle physics and to statistical mechanics. Enrico Fermi died on 28 November 1954 in Chicago, Illinois, USA./||
 1901|"Kurt Otto Friedrichs":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/kurt-otto-friedrichs Kurt Otto Friedrichs was born on 28 September 1901 in Kiel, Germany. Kurt Friedrichs was a German American mathematician who worked on many aspects of partial differential equations. He was the co-founder of the Courant Institute. Kurt Otto Friedrichs died on 31 December 1982 in New Rochelle, New York, USA./||
 1901|"Semyon Aranovich Gershgorin":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/semyon-aranovich-gershgorin Semyon Aranovich Gershgorin was born on 24 August 1901 in Pruzhany, Belarus. Semyon Aranovich Gershgorin died on 30 May 1933 in Leningrad, now St Petersburg, Russia./||
 1901|"Richard Lloyd Gwilt":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/richard-lloyd-gwilt Richard Lloyd Gwilt was born on 25 July 1901 in Edinburgh, Scotland. Richard Gwilt was an actuary who worked for various Edinburgh insurance companies. He was a Fellow of the Faculty of Actuaries and of the Institute of Actuaries. Richard Lloyd Gwilt died on 21 August 1972 in Edinburgh, Scotland./||
 1901|"Werner Karl Heisenberg":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/werner-karl-heisenberg Werner Karl Heisenberg was born on 5 December 1901 in Würzburg, Germany. Werner Heisenberg did important work in Quantum Mechanics as well as nuclear physics. Werner Karl Heisenberg died on 1 February 1976 in Munich, Germany./||
 1901|"Nikolai Evgrafovich Kochin":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/nikolai-evgrafovich-kochin Nikolai Evgrafovich Kochin was born on 6 May 1901 in St Petersburg, Russia. Nikolai Evgrafovich Kochin died on 31 December 1944 in Moscow, USSR./||
 1901|"Ugo Morin":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/ugo-morin Ugo Morin was born on 7 February 1901 in Trieste, Austrian Empire (now Italy). Ugo Morin died on 1 January 1968 in Padua, Italy./||
 1901|"Petr Sergeevich Novikov":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/petr-sergeevich-novikov Petr Sergeevich Novikov was born on 15 August 1901 in Moscow, Russia. Petr Sergeevich Novikov is a Russian mathematician known for his work on combinatorial problems in group theory including the word problem for groups and the Burnside problem. Petr Sergeevich Novikov died on 9 January 1975 in Moscow, Russia./||
 1901|"Kiyoshi Oka":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/kiyoshi-oka Kiyoshi Oka was born on 19 April 1901 in Osaka, Wakayama Prefecture, Japan. Kiyoshi Oka died on 1 March 1978 in Nara, Japan./||
 1901|"Ivan Georgievich Petrovsky":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/ivan-georgievich-petrovsky Ivan Georgievich Petrovsky was born on 18 January 1901 in Sevsk, Orlov guberniya, Russia. Ivan Petrovsky was a Russian mathematician who worked in the field of partial differential equations. Ivan Georgievich Petrovsky died on 15 January 1973 in Moscow, USSR./||
 1901|"Richard Alexander Robb":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/richard-alexander-robb Richard Alexander Robb was born on 7 September 1901 in Glasgow, Scotland. Richard Robb studied at Glasgow and Michigan universities. Most of his career was spent at Glasgow University lecturing on Mathematics and Statistics. Richard Alexander Robb died on 22 March 1977 in Eaglesham, Renfrewshire, Scotland./||
 1901|"Friedrich Karl Schmidt":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/friedrich-karl-schmidt Friedrich Karl Schmidt was born on 22 September 1901 in Düsseldorf, Germany. Friedrich Karl Schmidt died on e"25 January 1977 in Heidelberg, Germany./||
 1901|"Otto Schreier":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/otto-schreier Otto Schreier was born on 3 March 1901 in Vienna, Austria. Schreier worked in combinatorial group theory, particularly on subgroups of free groups and on knot groups. Otto Schreier died on 2 June 1929 in Hamburg, Germany./||
 1901|"Mary Constance Simpson":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/mary-constance-simpson Mary Constance Simpson was born 1901 in Gateshead-on-Tyne, England. Mary Simpson graduated from Edinburgh and then took up a post at Queen's College Dundee. Her date and place of of death is unknown./||
 1901|"Alfred Tarski":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/alfred-tarski Alfred Tarski was born on 14 January 1901 in Warsaw during the 3rd partition of Poland in the Russian zone. Tarski made important contributions in many areas of mathematics, including metamathematics, set theory, measure theory, model theory, and general algebra. Alfred Tarski died on 26 October 1983 in Berkeley, California, USA./||
 1901|"George Frederick James Temple":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/george-frederick-james-temple George Frederick James Temple was born on 1 September 1901 in Kensington, London, England. George Frederick James Temple died on 30 January 1992 in Quarr Abbey, Isle of Wight, England./||
 1901|"Steven Vajda":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/steven-vajda Steven Vajda was born on 20 August 1901 in Budapest, Hungary. Steven Vajda died on 10 December 1995 in Brighton, Sussex, England./||
 1901|"William Marvin Whyburn":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/william-marvin-whyburn William Marvin Whyburn was born on 12 November 1901 in Lewisville, Denton County, Texas, USA. William Marvin Whyburn died on 5 May 1972 in Greenville, North Carolina, USA./||
 1901|"John Williamson":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/john-williamson John Williamson was born on 23 May 1901 in Kinross, Scotland. John Williamson graduated from Edinburgh University and then had an appointment at St Andrews. He spent some time in Chicago and eventually moved to the USA to a post at Johns Hopkins University in Baltimore. His most important work was in Algebra. John Williamson died in 1949 in Baltimore, USA./||
 1901|"Édouard Zeckendorf":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/edouard-zeckendorf Édouard Zeckendorf was born on 2 May 1901 in Liège, Belgium. Édouard Zeckendorf died on 16 May 1983 in Liège, Belgium./||
 1902|"Reinhold Baer":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/reinhold-baer Reinhold Baer was born on 22 July 1902 in Berlin, Germany. Baer's mathematical work was wide ranging; topology, abelian groups and geometry. His most important work, however, was in group theory, on the extension problem for groups, finiteness conditions, soluble and nilpotent groups. Reinhold Baer died on 22 October 1979 in Zürich, Switzerland./||
 1902|"Gheorghe Calugăreănu":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/gheorghe-calugareanu Gheorghe Calugăreănu was born on 16 July 1902 in Iasi, Romania. Gheorghe Calugăreănu died on 15 November 1976 in Cluj, Romania./||
 1902|"Stefan Emmanuilovich Cohn-Vossen":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/stefan-emmanuilovich-cohn-vossen Stefan Emmanuilovich Cohn-Vossen was born on 28 May 1902 in Breslau, Germany, now Wroclaw, Poland. Stefan Emmanuilovich Cohn-Vossen died on 25 June 1936 in Moscow, Russia./||
 1902|"Paul Adrien Maurice Dirac":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/paul-adrien-maurice-dirac Paul Adrien Maurice Dirac was born on 8 August 1902 in Bristol, England. Dirac is famous as the creator of the complete theoretical formulation of quantum mechanics. Paul Adrien Maurice Dirac died on 20 October 1984 in Tallahassee, Florida, USA./||
 1902|"Wallace John Eckert":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/wallace-john-eckert Wallace John Eckert was born on 19 June 1902 in Pittsburgh, Pennsylvania, USA. Wallace John Eckert died on 24 August 1971 in Englewood, New Jersey, USA./||
 1902|"Theodor Estermann":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/theodor-estermann Theodor Estermann was born on 5 February 1902 in Neubrandenburg, Germany. Theodor Estermann died on 29 November 1991 in London, England./||
 1902|"Gilbert Leslie Frewin":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/gilbert-leslie-frewin Gilbert Leslie Frewin was born on 6 September 1902 in Glasgow, Scotland. Leslie Frewin graduated from the University of Edinburgh and taught at George Watson's College before moving to Inverness. Gilbert Leslie Frewin died in 1999 in Leicester, England./||
 1902|"Stanislaw Golab":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/stanislaw-golab Stanislaw Golab was born on 26 July 1902 in Travnik, Bosnia, Austro-Hungarian Empire. Stanislaw Golab died on 26 April 1980 in Kraków, Poland./||
 1902|"Marion Cameron Gray":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/marion-cameron-gray Marion Cameron Gray was born on 26 March 1902 in Ayr, Scotland. Marion Gray graduated from Edinburgh University and then went to Bryn Mawr College in the USA. She completed her doctorate there and returned to posts at Edinburgh and Imperial College London. She returned to the USA and worked for AT&amp;T; for the rest of her career. The Gray graph is named after her. Marion Cameron Gray died on 16 September 1979 in Edinburgh, Scotland./||
 1902|"Wolfgang Siegfried Haack":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/wolfgang-siegfried-haack Wolfgang Siegfried Haack was born on 24 April 1902 in Gotha, Thuringia, Germany. Wolfgang Siegfried Haack died on 28 November 1994 in Berlin, Germany./||
 1902|"Eberhard Frederich Ferdinand Hopf":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/eberhard-frederich-ferdinand-hopf Eberhard Frederich Ferdinand Hopf was born on 4 April 1902 in Salzburg, Austria. Eberhard Frederich Ferdinand Hopf died on 24 July 1983./||
 1902|"Edna Ernestine Kramer":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/edna-ernestine-kramer-lassar Edna Ernestine Kramer Lassar was born on 11 May 1902 in Manhattan, New York, USA. Edna Ernestine Kramer Lassar died on 9 July 1984 in Manhattan, New York, USA./||
 1902|"Karl Menger":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/karl-menger Karl Menger was born on 13 January 1902 in Vienna, Austria. Karl Menger was an Austrian-American mathematician who worked on algebras, geometries, curve and dimension theory. He also contributed to game theory and social sciences. Karl Menger died on 5 October 1985 in Chicago, Illinois, USA./||

 1902|"Hans Wilhelm Eduard Schwerdtfeger":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/hans-wilhelm-eduard-schwerdtfeger Hans Wilhelm Eduard Schwerdtfeger was born on 9 December 1902 in Göttingen, Germany. Hans Wilhelm Eduard Schwerdtfeger died on 26 June 1990 in Adelaide, Australia./||
 1902|"Kenjiro Shoda":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/kenjiro-shoda Kenjiro Shoda was born on 25 February 1902 in Tatebayashi, Gunma Prefecture, Japan. Kenjiro Shoda died on 20 March 1977 in Ashikaga, Japan./||
 1902|"Abraham Wald":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/abraham-wald Abraham Wald was born on 31 October 1902 in Kolozsvár, Hungary (now Cluj, Romania). Abraham Wald was a mathematician born in what is now Romania who worked on decision theory, geometry and econometrics. Abraham Wald died on 13 December 1950 in Travancore, India./||

 1902|"Eugene Paul Wigner":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/eugene-paul-wigner Eugene Paul Wigner was born on 17 November 1902 in Budapest, Hungary. Eugene Paul Wigner was a Hungarian-American theoretical physicist and mathematician who won a Nobel prize for his contributions to the theory of the atomic nucleus and elementary particles. Eugene Paul Wigner died on 1 January 1995 in Princeton, New Jersey, USA./||

 1903|"Zygmunt William Birnbaum":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/zygmunt-william-birnbaum Zygmunt William Birnbaum was born on 18 October 1903 in Lemberg, Austrian Empire (now Lviv, Ukraine). Zygmunt William Birnbaum died on 15 December 2000 in Seattle, USA./||
 1903|"Lancelot Stephen Bosanquet":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/lancelot-stephen-bosanquet Lancelot Stephen Bosanquet was born on 26 December 1903 in St. Stephen's-by-Saltash, Cornwall, England. Lancelot Stephen Bosanquet died on 10 January 1984 in Cambridge, Cambridgeshire, England./||
 1903|"Thomas Arthur Alan Broadbent":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/thomas-arthur-alan-broadbent Thomas Arthur Alan Broadbent was born on 31 May 1903 in Consett, County Durham, England. Thomas Arthur Alan Broadbent died on 27 January 1973 in Greenwich, England./||
 1903|"Alonzo Church":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/alonzo-church Alonzo Church was born on 14 June 1903 in Washington, D.C., USA. Alonzo Church made important contributions to mathematical logic and theoretical computer science. Alonzo Church died on 11 August 1995 in Hudson, Ohio, USA./||
 1903|"Georges de Rham":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/georges-de-rham Georges de Rham was born on 10 September 1903 in Roche, Canton Vaud, Switzerland. Georges de Rham was a Swiss mathematician, known for his contributions to differential topology and to algebraic topology. Georges de Rham died on 9 October 1990 in Lausanne, Switzerland./||
 1903|"Jean Frédéric Auguste Delsarte":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/jean-frederic-auguste-delsarte Jean Frédéric Auguste Delsarte was born on 19 October 1903 in Fourmies (Nord), France. Jean Delsarte was a French mathematician known for his work in mathematical analysis. Jean Frédéric Auguste Delsarte died on 28 November 1968 in Nancy, France./||
 1903|"Irmgard Flügge-Lotz":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/irmgard-fluegge-lotz Irmgard Flügge-Lotz was born on 16 July 1903 in Hameln, Germany. Irmgard Flügge-Lotz worked on numerical methods for solving differential equations especially in fluid dynamics. Irmgard Flügge-Lotz died on 22 May 1974 in Stanford, USA./||
 1903|"Robert Pollock Gillespie":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/robert-pollock-gillespie Robert Pollock Gillespie was born on 21 November 1903 in Johnstone, Renfrewshire, Scotland. Robert Gillespie studied at Glasgow and Cambridge and then lectured at Glasgow University. His main interests were in analysis. Robert Pollock Gillespie died on 1 January 1977 in Edzell, Angus, Scotland./||
 1903|"Sydney Goldstein":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/sydney-goldstein Sydney Goldstein was born on 3 December 1903 in Hull, England. Sydney Goldstein died on 22 January 1989 in Brockton, Massachusetts, USA./||
 1903|"William Vallance Douglas Hodge":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/william-vallance-douglas-hodge William Vallance Douglas Hodge was born on 17 June 1903 in Edinburgh, Scotland. William Hodge was Lowndean Professor of Astronomy and Geometry at Cambridge. His main interests were in Algebraic Geometry and Differential Geometry. William Vallance Douglas Hodge died on 7 July 1975 in Cambridge, Cambridgeshire, England./||
 1903|"Bertha Swirles Jeffreys":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/bertha-swirles-jeffreys Bertha Swirles Jeffreys was born on 22 May 1903 in Northampton, England. Bertha Swirles Jeffreys died on 18 December 1999 in Cambridge, England./||
 1903|"Andrey Nikolaevich Kolmogorov":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/andrey-nikolaevich-kolmogorov Andrey Nikolaevich Kolmogorov was born on 25 April 1903 in Tambov, Tambov province, Russia. Kolmogorov was one of the developers of probability theory. He later used this work to study the motion of the planets and the turbulent flow of air from a jet engine. Andrey Nikolaevich Kolmogorov died on 20 October 1987 in Moscow, Russia./||
 1903|"Dudley Ernest Littlewood":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/dudley-ernest-littlewood Dudley Ernest Littlewood was born on 7 September 1903 in London, England. Dudley Ernest Littlewood died on 6 October 1979 in Llandudno, Wales./||
 1903|"Gladys Isabel Mackenzie":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/gladys-isabel-mackenzie Gladys Isabel Mackenzie was born on 2 May 1903 in Edinburgh, Scotland. Gladys Mackenzie graduated from the University of Edinburgh and became an assistant in the Natural Philosophy department. She moved to Newnham College Cambridge and late to Bristol University and Queen Elizabeth College London. She published papers on X-ray spectroscopy. Gladys Isabel Mackenzie died in After 1972 in London, England./||
 1903|"Kurt Mahler":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/kurt-mahler Kurt Mahler was born on 26 July 1903 in Krefeld, Prussian Rhineland. Kurt Mahler was a German mathematician who made important contributions to the theory of transcendental numbers. Kurt Mahler died on 25 February 1988 in Canberra, Australia./||

 1903|"John von Neumann":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/john-von-neumann John von Neumann was born on 28 December 1903 in Budapest, Hungary. Von Neumann built a solid framework for quantum mechanics. He also worked in game theory, studied what are now called von Neumann Algebras, and was one of the pioneers of computer science. John von Neumann died on 8 February 1957 in Washington D.C., USA./||

 1903|"Howard Percy Robertson":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/howard-percy-robertson Howard Percy Robertson was born on 27 January 1903 in Hoquiam, Washington, USA. Howard Percy Robertson studied at Washington University and California Institute of Technology. He spent some time in Germany and was appointed to a post in Princeton. He spent much of the period of World War II in Britain. He made important contributions to Differential Geometry and Relativity. Howard Percy Robertson died on 26 August 1961./||

She taught for some time at a Horticultural College in Kent before returning to the USA. Catherine Cassels Steele died on 3 December 1995 in Lacy, Washington, USA./||

 1906|"Thomas George Cowling":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/thomas-george-cowling Thomas George Cowling was born on 17 June 1906 in Hackney, London, England. Tom Cowling graduated from Oxford and worked at Imperial College London. He lectured at Swansea, Dundee and Manchester and became a professor at Bangor and Leeds. He worked on theoretical astronomy and stellar physics. Thomas George Cowling died on 16 June 1990 in Leeds, England./||

Dieudonné was a French mathematician who worked in a wide variety of mathematical areas including general topology, topological vector spaces, algebraic geometry, invariant theory and the classical groups. He was a founder member of Bourbaki and also wrote on the history of mathematics. Jean Alexandre Eugène Dieudonné died on 29 November 1992 in Paris, France./||

 1906|"Kurt Gödel":https://www.bookofproofs.org/history/kurt-goedel Kurt Gödel was born on 28 April 1906 in Brünn, Austria-Hungary (now Brno, Czech Republic). Gödel proved fundamental results about axiomatic systems showing in any axiomatic mathematical system there are propositions that cannot be proved or disproved within the axioms of the system. Kurt Gödel died on 14 January 1978 in Princeton, New Jersey, USA./||
